msg:It should be the best hotel in Kashgar. The room temperature was 29-30 degrees. The waiter installed an electric fan, but I still couldn't sleep all night. I asked help to adjust the temperature before going out in the afternoon. When I came back in the evening, it was still very hot. The luggage was already packed in the room, and I was finally told that I could change rooms, but it was already 1 a.m., and I flew out the next morning. Xinjiang is beautiful and the people are very welcoming, but Radisson's brand and price are really not suitable for Kashgar. BTW, the service level also needs to be greatly improved. There are no waiters to carry luggage. More and more people are traveling to Xinjiang, and they also need well-known hotel brands, and they can really improve their service quality. Don't hold back Xinjiang's tourism industry!

I have never seen such a bad five-star hotel.
